<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="939e0d9fa12e4789b1759e5ed44effe1"><span data-offset-key="939e0d9fa12e4789b1759e5ed44effe1:0">`cibuildwheel`</span><span data-offset-key="939e0d9fa12e4789b1759e5ed44effe1:1"> is a Python package that builds </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Wheel" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="02d54df0be634d0b929aefec758c5215"><span data-offset-key="02d54df0be634d0b929aefec758c5215:0">wheels</span></span></a><span data-key="6716e8135b70440592e87420c63a6be6"><span data-offset-key="6716e8135b70440592e87420c63a6be6:0"> for all common platforms and Python versions on most CI systems. Also see </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#multibuild" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ea364ade3aab44f0bf0aff71b2ef672f"><span data-offset-key="ea364ade3aab44f0bf0aff71b2ef672f:0">multibuild</span></span></a><span data-key="c5d66a20f01941c2a1d6a73db9e78bcd"><span data-offset-key="c5d66a20f01941c2a1d6a73db9e78bcd:0">.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5bc5e39162c34b5e8c424c3c68469e59"><span data-offset-key="5bc5e39162c34b5e8c424c3c68469e59:0">distlib</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#distlib" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a8673be13f69429ab27f17b24810633c"><span data-offset-key="a8673be13f69429ab27f17b24810633c:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="6109a1be50dd48c795bf59c2e8258764"><span data-offset-key="6109a1be50dd48c795bf59c2e8258764:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="79cd829c947e4226b2c00eee14059181"><span data-offset-key="79cd829c947e4226b2c00eee14059181:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="http://pythonhosted.org/distlib/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="65d587e72ae74c8ea3aa24ca80561106"><span data-offset-key="65d587e72ae74c8ea3aa24ca80561106:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="c3a6b3b7c5e941db9d9ad270f76c54eb"><span data-offset-key="c3a6b3b7c5e941db9d9ad270f76c54eb:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://bitbucket.org/pypa/distlib/issues?status=new&amp;status=open" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="86166776633341b098a19476ab7eb4e3"><span data-offset-key="86166776633341b098a19476ab7eb4e3:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="437e45c9177e446dbf7338fdc4b333be"><span data-offset-key="437e45c9177e446dbf7338fdc4b333be:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://bitbucket.org/pypa/distlib" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c01eff707eb647db8f956bae5b5d67fb"><span data-offset-key="c01eff707eb647db8f956bae5b5d67fb:0">Bitbucket</span></span></a><span data-key="291d1445c5024219898cf4964ea3e49a"><span data-offset-key="291d1445c5024219898cf4964ea3e49a:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/distlib" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8419c6995ea94296ae38360f89e9790d"><span data-offset-key="8419c6995ea94296ae38360f89e9790d:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="c102c5ac53b348ea9d1812dbf5ce81f5"><span data-offset-key="c102c5ac53b348ea9d1812dbf5ce81f5:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="57774ff3ef95468bbae2091b9c54d982"><span data-offset-key="57774ff3ef95468bbae2091b9c54d982:0">`distlib`</span><span data-offset-key="57774ff3ef95468bbae2091b9c54d982:1"> is a library which implements low-level functions that relate to packaging and distribution of Python software. </span><span data-offset-key="57774ff3ef95468bbae2091b9c54d982:2">`distlib`</span><span data-offset-key="57774ff3ef95468bbae2091b9c54d982:3"> implements several relevant PEPs (Python Enhancement Proposal standards) and is useful for developers of third-party packaging tools to make and upload binary and source </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="df468a8ceb2b431680dfb1f4417d809a"><span data-offset-key="df468a8ceb2b431680dfb1f4417d809a:0">distributions</span></span></a><span data-key="54ecfadf6a6147bfacde5010c84b187f"><span data-offset-key="54ecfadf6a6147bfacde5010c84b187f:0">, achieve interoperability, resolve dependencies, manage package resources, and do other similar functions.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="088ebdbfb08b45b1ac3535940ecd7ce6"><span data-offset-key="088ebdbfb08b45b1ac3535940ecd7ce6:0">Unlike the stricter </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#packaging" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0d87ba80d9a5481da07ea26bf1176409"><span data-offset-key="0d87ba80d9a5481da07ea26bf1176409:0">packaging</span></span></a><span data-key="91a287476e2e49aa946ee591a025b699"><span data-offset-key="91a287476e2e49aa946ee591a025b699:0"> project (below), which specifically implements modern Python packaging interoperability standards, </span><span data-offset-key="91a287476e2e49aa946ee591a025b699:1">`distlib`</span><span data-offset-key="91a287476e2e49aa946ee591a025b699:2"> also attempts to provide reasonable fallback behaviours when asked to handle legacy packages and metadata that predate the modern interoperability standards and fall into the subset of packages that are incompatible with those standards.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="981f0917694d4977b40efcd6cafdcec4"><span data-offset-key="981f0917694d4977b40efcd6cafdcec4:0">packaging</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#packaging" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="47b7126df57847e695553e43d136af4e"><span data-offset-key="47b7126df57847e695553e43d136af4e:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="0c42aa9abc554dfb9abc044144e0654c"><span data-offset-key="0c42aa9abc554dfb9abc044144e0654c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6bb59b30e6a14404854f8ca6c517a8d2"><span data-offset-key="6bb59b30e6a14404854f8ca6c517a8d2:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://packaging.pypa.io/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d278688901034de499b75b7ba46b2732"><span data-offset-key="d278688901034de499b75b7ba46b2732:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="6994e1427c9c43559a133385e762e561"><span data-offset-key="6994e1427c9c43559a133385e762e561:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/packaging/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1b3498fea2f14ff89e9bfaa5d7cf9aaf"><span data-offset-key="1b3498fea2f14ff89e9bfaa5d7cf9aaf:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="b948142b8b1746b4bf95b1985a4b26e8"><span data-offset-key="b948142b8b1746b4bf95b1985a4b26e8:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/packaging" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5c71fe1fc3484140a62d3630119010be"><span data-offset-key="5c71fe1fc3484140a62d3630119010be:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="a6653a2e9fc84cb48c0365a8b8cc9694"><span data-offset-key="a6653a2e9fc84cb48c0365a8b8cc9694:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/packaging" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6161a1af5e814ece8cf79b4562a3f950"><span data-offset-key="6161a1af5e814ece8cf79b4562a3f950:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="8656c535fcd446289a230d4833730170"><span data-offset-key="8656c535fcd446289a230d4833730170:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9e33cf1b70124053a146264faf83c8cf"><span data-offset-key="9e33cf1b70124053a146264faf83c8cf:0">Core utilities for Python packaging used by </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="006ea43c86ee471795475223aa309235"><span data-offset-key="006ea43c86ee471795475223aa309235:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="8a3ee6b0e0374405a6ce50b4bcf0ef0d"><span data-offset-key="8a3ee6b0e0374405a6ce50b4bcf0ef0d:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="891f9d2db85a47b4a77acf5339a18b34"><span data-offset-key="891f9d2db85a47b4a77acf5339a18b34:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="0fe3da0d36dd4647a63fa38e45b47c9e"><span data-offset-key="0fe3da0d36dd4647a63fa38e45b47c9e:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="99b1264649404e4e95d817431ca58689"><span data-offset-key="99b1264649404e4e95d817431ca58689:0">The core utilities in the packaging library handle version handling, specifiers, markers, requirements, tags, and similar attributes and tasks for Python packages. Most Python users rely on this library without needing to explicitly call it; developers of the other Python packaging, distribution, and installation tools listed here often use its functionality to parse, discover, and otherwise handle dependency attributes.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="114d2c8323ec45d69f4a2ec17139231e"><span data-offset-key="114d2c8323ec45d69f4a2ec17139231e:0">This project specifically focuses on implementing the modern Python packaging interoperability standards defined at </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/specifications/#packaging-specifications" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fb613e7a84524b27b581463c704f7a09"><span data-offset-key="fb613e7a84524b27b581463c704f7a09:0">PyPA specifications</span></span></a><span data-key="6d7d70777bd94ec7ba17cd4c2d055035"><span data-offset-key="6d7d70777bd94ec7ba17cd4c2d055035:0">, and will report errors for sufficiently old legacy packages that are incompatible with those standards. In contrast, the </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#distlib" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e1fa94398ab5487290c74f30948b1c71"><span data-offset-key="e1fa94398ab5487290c74f30948b1c71:0">distlib</span></span></a><span data-key="3e8d04c864ae4696b0c0c8d33d8fd282"><span data-offset-key="3e8d04c864ae4696b0c0c8d33d8fd282:0"> project is a more permissive library that attempts to provide a plausible reading of ambiguous metadata in cases where </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#packaging" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1f80a25c2cdb407cb772e46c43277023"><span data-offset-key="1f80a25c2cdb407cb772e46c43277023:0">packaging</span></span></a><span data-key="8188ff317c8f4f629c2e1f961ce3e289"><span data-offset-key="8188ff317c8f4f629c2e1f961ce3e289:0"> will instead report on error.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b583d034f244f23997b9a02eed6cb58"><span data-offset-key="9b583d034f244f23997b9a02eed6cb58:0">pip</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1e75c22c62694fae8884dafb8ce17869"><span data-offset-key="1e75c22c62694fae8884dafb8ce17869:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="84a2d2c0941e4ee6b2b1589ee851641e"><span data-offset-key="84a2d2c0941e4ee6b2b1589ee851641e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="eb8cba4d21774c6984088f2b2f4b9585"><span data-offset-key="eb8cba4d21774c6984088f2b2f4b9585:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pip.pypa.io/en/stable/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a3e00d90144f4b8f8d7060bfc7458c77"><span data-offset-key="a3e00d90144f4b8f8d7060bfc7458c77:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="8e61645ed50e49f78834339e8e1cb820"><span data-offset-key="8e61645ed50e49f78834339e8e1cb820:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2ef2cfe5604c46669dd72cdec087a493"><span data-offset-key="2ef2cfe5604c46669dd72cdec087a493:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="10d68b5862b946839951df9674dfa7b8"><span data-offset-key="10d68b5862b946839951df9674dfa7b8:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="130f2be3e7ef406d8fa373cad125a0a3"><span data-offset-key="130f2be3e7ef406d8fa373cad125a0a3:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="f7079481c71f4230af56ab818f241d46"><span data-offset-key="f7079481c71f4230af56ab818f241d46:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/pip/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="90afb9362bc44282a533b6b784afdb84"><span data-offset-key="90afb9362bc44282a533b6b784afdb84:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="0601a3f370b747129afde25876c6fcab"><span data-offset-key="0601a3f370b747129afde25876c6fcab:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c06b1bde8fc24f01aa0f3b3e6da9b68b"><span data-offset-key="c06b1bde8fc24f01aa0f3b3e6da9b68b:0">The most popular tool for installing Python packages, and the one included with modern versions of Python.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d0de0a6155864140b540540fd6df55bf"><span data-offset-key="d0de0a6155864140b540540fd6df55bf:0">It provides the essential core features for finding, downloading, and installing packages from PyPI and other Python package indexes, and can be incorporated into a wide range of development workflows via its command-line interface (CLI).</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="22d09ae6d9c645009917b2d83482fc23"><span data-offset-key="22d09ae6d9c645009917b2d83482fc23:0">Pipenv</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pipenv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d4beef21eb8e4d83b69c6d367ff8f381"><span data-offset-key="d4beef21eb8e4d83b69c6d367ff8f381:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="65c60646c82444bd8a01ebcf81941ba6"><span data-offset-key="65c60646c82444bd8a01ebcf81941ba6:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="641731e765144bb1b90cfd654e11dd26"><span data-offset-key="641731e765144bb1b90cfd654e11dd26:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pipenv.pypa.io/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3df6d03a05d5495c89b5bc533dc2bad1"><span data-offset-key="3df6d03a05d5495c89b5bc533dc2bad1:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="f03d76245ba948e49d3ee4fdcc0807ba"><span data-offset-key="f03d76245ba948e49d3ee4fdcc0807ba:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/pipenv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5e31f96f49304868b390a16747adc669"><span data-offset-key="5e31f96f49304868b390a16747adc669:0">Source</span></span></a><span data-key="6d06c82a7c6b4de792ef5953f09fbf92"><span data-offset-key="6d06c82a7c6b4de792ef5953f09fbf92:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/pipenv/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cddffa6bdd2b410f9e32aead2771ada0"><span data-offset-key="cddffa6bdd2b410f9e32aead2771ada0:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="d70f743d94494a4bbc5a574589923cf6"><span data-offset-key="d70f743d94494a4bbc5a574589923cf6:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/pipenv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d9d8b1303e1748a68c9e06d167feb210"><span data-offset-key="d9d8b1303e1748a68c9e06d167feb210:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="57f59e49af86445193e7d46530571755"><span data-offset-key="57f59e49af86445193e7d46530571755:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bd78da8841844436a0e3b34bc9152580"><span data-offset-key="bd78da8841844436a0e3b34bc9152580:0">Pipenv is a project that aims to bring the best of all packaging worlds to the Python world. It harnesses </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pipfile" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="544b80fb7e534b0481f4db21b6e11979"><span data-offset-key="544b80fb7e534b0481f4db21b6e11979:0">Pipfile</span></span></a><span data-key="f7e89faeb0cd475385183418c987b7cd"><span data-offset-key="f7e89faeb0cd475385183418c987b7cd:0">, </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b16a0baed3064bf9a081f0915bf23ab2"><span data-offset-key="b16a0baed3064bf9a081f0915bf23ab2:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="afeec690cbe744f59f4eb14c04586df9"><span data-offset-key="afeec690cbe744f59f4eb14c04586df9:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#virtualenv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5f1e94d8373d499e99626a335d28da67"><span data-offset-key="5f1e94d8373d499e99626a335d28da67:0">virtualenv</span></span></a><span data-key="6a6a2444ee7c4946843911515557318b"><span data-offset-key="6a6a2444ee7c4946843911515557318b:0"> into one single toolchain. It features very pretty terminal colors.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8fc0ec61824b47b1a8b7ed16a4dae1ef"><span data-offset-key="8fc0ec61824b47b1a8b7ed16a4dae1ef:0">Pipenv aims to help users manage environments, dependencies, and imported packages on the command line. It also works well on Windows (which other tools often underserve), makes and checkes file hashes, to ensure compliance with hash-locked dependency specifiers, and eases uninstallation of packages and dependencies. It is used by Python users and system administrators, but has been less maintained since late 2018.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5c7cd6f27c0a4af2b2769b382d6fe103"><span data-offset-key="5c7cd6f27c0a4af2b2769b382d6fe103:0">Pipfile</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pipfile" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a88ca34a055e4a549b028aae79f78510"><span data-offset-key="a88ca34a055e4a549b028aae79f78510:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="8af3a6324d8548a094f77a2186d1abae"><span data-offset-key="8af3a6324d8548a094f77a2186d1abae:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2d094f6bf4ae4b21bdc29f67b6847a70"><span data-offset-key="2d094f6bf4ae4b21bdc29f67b6847a70:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/pipfile" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f3ef5a81e0664788ae10003d8afb0681"><span data-offset-key="f3ef5a81e0664788ae10003d8afb0681:0">Source</span></span></a><span data-key="efbe581dc4724ff7aa671b6330f288fa"><span data-offset-key="efbe581dc4724ff7aa671b6330f288fa:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="027e6d213619416c97a50b248f87c233"><span data-offset-key="027e6d213619416c97a50b248f87c233:0">`Pipfile`</span><span data-offset-key="027e6d213619416c97a50b248f87c233:1"> and its sister </span><span data-offset-key="027e6d213619416c97a50b248f87c233:2">`Pipfile.lock`</span><span data-offset-key="027e6d213619416c97a50b248f87c233:3"> are a higher-level application-centric alternative to </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="aa2aa01ac92b4408a74b45bb4c936a3e"><span data-offset-key="aa2aa01ac92b4408a74b45bb4c936a3e:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="6f65b6e018484cde933af2636e1b44ec"><span data-offset-key="6f65b6e018484cde933af2636e1b44ec:0">’s lower-level </span><span data-offset-key="6f65b6e018484cde933af2636e1b44ec:1">`requirements.txt`</span><span data-offset-key="6f65b6e018484cde933af2636e1b44ec:2"> file.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c8883d2705644954a86d12fdb76791ba"><span data-offset-key="c8883d2705644954a86d12fdb76791ba:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pypa.github.io/pipx/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4e41d2dedeeb4f3daa5b126258798e38"><span data-offset-key="4e41d2dedeeb4f3daa5b126258798e38:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="cda67b81a4d5462e883bdfff51c3d319"><span data-offset-key="cda67b81a4d5462e883bdfff51c3d319:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/pipx" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="54636dfd1b86424995c4a29f53812019"><span data-offset-key="54636dfd1b86424995c4a29f53812019:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="59a31095aa284ff0af4e5f5d5a06c657"><span data-offset-key="59a31095aa284ff0af4e5f5d5a06c657:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/pipx/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="76bdc4886ab0427993de24c156b1c2c4"><span data-offset-key="76bdc4886ab0427993de24c156b1c2c4:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="c26de80c89c345d09a57b1633bc41ec3"><span data-offset-key="c26de80c89c345d09a57b1633bc41ec3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7253ec3a54ae4d89a6e254d2b8904105"><span data-offset-key="7253ec3a54ae4d89a6e254d2b8904105:0">pipx is a tool to install and run Python command-line applications without causing dependency conflicts with other packages installed on the system.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="dea8f1a791d9447abf87dba9eb4a1cc0"><span data-offset-key="dea8f1a791d9447abf87dba9eb4a1cc0:0">readme_renderer</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#readme-renderer" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="344b3e70a1d54640bae73cab65db6e3d"><span data-offset-key="344b3e70a1d54640bae73cab65db6e3d:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="0228ca2cc08f4e0ea34a71fa2a8863e8"><span data-offset-key="0228ca2cc08f4e0ea34a71fa2a8863e8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4a02528676b840a7b02dd43b9ddefb05"><span data-offset-key="4a02528676b840a7b02dd43b9ddefb05:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/readme_renderer/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f87097e0ed2848ad9114ae3b1fdf3569"><span data-offset-key="f87097e0ed2848ad9114ae3b1fdf3569:0">GitHub and docs</span></span></a><span data-key="6d56092afe9e4a51b1f533707bf47463"><span data-offset-key="6d56092afe9e4a51b1f533707bf47463:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/readme_renderer/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="517c0f5bd6b24484b1abd405d0e8db5c"><span data-offset-key="517c0f5bd6b24484b1abd405d0e8db5c:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="604a39a2ceed44ea8c9e4830b708fa24"><span data-offset-key="604a39a2ceed44ea8c9e4830b708fa24:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0f6a05764b1e4be8b4113578d8a0982f"><span data-offset-key="0f6a05764b1e4be8b4113578d8a0982f:0">`readme_renderer`</span><span data-offset-key="0f6a05764b1e4be8b4113578d8a0982f:1"> is a library that package developers use to render their user documentation (README) files into HTML from markup languages such as Markdown or reStructuredText. Developers call it on its own or via </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#twine" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="06e741013c94470f9947de87b2bcf2eb"><span data-offset-key="06e741013c94470f9947de87b2bcf2eb:0">twine</span></span></a><span data-key="ed1b02e4a13f48df90c0708a02df668a"><span data-offset-key="ed1b02e4a13f48df90c0708a02df668a:0">, as part of their release management process, to check that their package descriptions will properly display on PyPI.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4e7a549a2a62499186ef133a358426ce"><span data-offset-key="4e7a549a2a62499186ef133a358426ce:0">setuptools</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#easy-install" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f8dc43dd2b7549e9a38a8d939fc1ba27"><span data-offset-key="f8dc43dd2b7549e9a38a8d939fc1ba27:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="9a54df5e26e04843bc4e4fdbcc9e36f9"><span data-offset-key="9a54df5e26e04843bc4e4fdbcc9e36f9:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4a0d57e3a39443099a5aef7998ba467c"><span data-offset-key="4a0d57e3a39443099a5aef7998ba467c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://setuptools.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8aa9e99261644602984e5bb947e7504c"><span data-offset-key="8aa9e99261644602984e5bb947e7504c:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="8faa85d0d82a464cb19e4ff7e557da1c"><span data-offset-key="8faa85d0d82a464cb19e4ff7e557da1c:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/setuptools/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e0292d942723442d8c1a7da20a6d3ce8"><span data-offset-key="e0292d942723442d8c1a7da20a6d3ce8:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="447c08ad587f445ea60f01e761925f16"><span data-offset-key="447c08ad587f445ea60f01e761925f16:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c0c6fac297904c90a4ff74a31b218193"><span data-offset-key="c0c6fac297904c90a4ff74a31b218193:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="011b7f7398f7424fa5c4ca212aa9053f"><span data-offset-key="011b7f7398f7424fa5c4ca212aa9053f:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cf26b1b81108420f8c66c666e3c5f9ad"><span data-offset-key="cf26b1b81108420f8c66c666e3c5f9ad:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="15727d097f6f43cfb2001f68dbcd4350"><span data-offset-key="15727d097f6f43cfb2001f68dbcd4350:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0ee797e348e345d2a886683e6fe2774d"><span data-offset-key="0ee797e348e345d2a886683e6fe2774d:0">setuptools (which includes </span><span data-offset-key="0ee797e348e345d2a886683e6fe2774d:1">`easy_install`</span><span data-offset-key="0ee797e348e345d2a886683e6fe2774d:2">) is a collection of enhancements to the Python distutils that allow you to more easily build and distribute Python </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7afd5623b9994378a160269aeb243407"><span data-offset-key="7afd5623b9994378a160269aeb243407:0">distributions</span></span></a><span data-key="3c94733de0694dd78c4058311bf9596e"><span data-offset-key="3c94733de0694dd78c4058311bf9596e:0">, especially ones that have dependencies on other packages.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9d3d65d737f94faaad4d74c2f47e2ef6"><span data-offset-key="9d3d65d737f94faaad4d74c2f47e2ef6:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/distribute" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="99d26163e3ab427a8a68ba24a42b0bf6"><span data-offset-key="99d26163e3ab427a8a68ba24a42b0bf6:0">distribute</span></span></a><span data-key="1f0d37357ab04529a4b0cb953d2005c9"><span data-offset-key="1f0d37357ab04529a4b0cb953d2005c9:0"> was a fork of setuptools that was merged back into setuptools (in v0.7), thereby making setuptools the primary choice for Python packaging.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6409264b02b443ecba9930329945a65b"><span data-offset-key="6409264b02b443ecba9930329945a65b:0">trove-classifiers</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#trove-classifiers" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b27bf035cfe54708a599cce1682a3098"><span data-offset-key="b27bf035cfe54708a599cce1682a3098:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="11db84f501fc48039813a3455b4da2bb"><span data-offset-key="11db84f501fc48039813a3455b4da2bb:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e2c7561557f049f0b902063af0069be8"><span data-offset-key="e2c7561557f049f0b902063af0069be8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/trove-classifiers/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0c02c60abb48469a9ba266fa87965538"><span data-offset-key="0c02c60abb48469a9ba266fa87965538:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="24a265c852dd48e0a4e495c9c74cf933"><span data-offset-key="24a265c852dd48e0a4e495c9c74cf933:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/trove-classifiers" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b33b9bd0bb0144eea62bfd18b479392d"><span data-offset-key="b33b9bd0bb0144eea62bfd18b479392d:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="2cb8f3b7263743699bcce992071e1538"><span data-offset-key="2cb8f3b7263743699bcce992071e1538:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/trove-classifiers/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c2a01aa90abb4354a1f34873fce7dd5f"><span data-offset-key="c2a01aa90abb4354a1f34873fce7dd5f:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="dac65c5b57d14bea848eb96d755b9c9d"><span data-offset-key="dac65c5b57d14bea848eb96d755b9c9d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d28ab386f3a246b4a8d233db555691b7"><span data-offset-key="d28ab386f3a246b4a8d233db555691b7:0">trove-classifiers is the canonical source for </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/classifiers/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6fd4df4e8bcd482ebcd69ccc54b10c80"><span data-offset-key="6fd4df4e8bcd482ebcd69ccc54b10c80:0">classifiers on PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="3c677c894eba404ca69e2778488cfb13"><span data-offset-key="3c677c894eba404ca69e2778488cfb13:0">, which project maintainers use to </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/specifications/core-metadata/#classifier-multiple-use" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1de24dad3d274ed6b30f7623c0c0280e"><span data-offset-key="1de24dad3d274ed6b30f7623c0c0280e:0">systematically describe their projects</span></span></a><span data-key="1ead50d14a4b43e0a16154766dcc00e3"><span data-offset-key="1ead50d14a4b43e0a16154766dcc00e3:0"> so that users can better find projects that match their needs on the PyPI.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="17b62f1f566e43899bf5d1b47b9f332f"><span data-offset-key="17b62f1f566e43899bf5d1b47b9f332f:0">The trove-classifiers package contains a list of valid classifiers and deprecated classifiers (which are paired with the classifiers that replace them). Use this package to validate classifiers used in packages intended for uploading to PyPI. As this list of classifiers is published as code, you can install and import it, giving you a more convenient workflow compared to referring to the </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/classifiers/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8aadc4953120479da1d4b48c93234c6d"><span data-offset-key="8aadc4953120479da1d4b48c93234c6d:0">list published on PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="b6b9ebcebd3e49fea3ebd552d2fb6c27"><span data-offset-key="b6b9ebcebd3e49fea3ebd552d2fb6c27:0">. The </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/trove-classifiers/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="63b0c027baf040cd8a276f70c492e5da"><span data-offset-key="63b0c027baf040cd8a276f70c492e5da:0">issue tracker</span></span></a><span data-key="5af381c06c7044d4917e54be896af184"><span data-offset-key="5af381c06c7044d4917e54be896af184:0"> for the project hosts discussions on proposed classifiers and requests for new classifiers.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="060cac9e1bfe4cb5a18da6d6aa742012"><span data-offset-key="060cac9e1bfe4cb5a18da6d6aa742012:0">twine</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#twine" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a95dc9fbe9a74b6294255ca36b29ae67"><span data-offset-key="a95dc9fbe9a74b6294255ca36b29ae67:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="a3069826948e4943918bfee60421b099"><span data-offset-key="a3069826948e4943918bfee60421b099:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bc9be4c8b6cb496aa5f70413c4d33e07"><span data-offset-key="bc9be4c8b6cb496aa5f70413c4d33e07:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://twine.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e6c0afea9e5e4a8aa4d42697ccd04a5a"><span data-offset-key="e6c0afea9e5e4a8aa4d42697ccd04a5a:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="c971fb0b04f04c0ab153ad2ab00548f5"><span data-offset-key="c971fb0b04f04c0ab153ad2ab00548f5:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/twine/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2794788743104e07b173f57f0c4ede8a"><span data-offset-key="2794788743104e07b173f57f0c4ede8a:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="8873f1b9b44a437e93bdaa2508be6d40"><span data-offset-key="8873f1b9b44a437e93bdaa2508be6d40:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/twine" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c87633cb628841448e69891e0381e2cb"><span data-offset-key="c87633cb628841448e69891e0381e2cb:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="0203a9325014488f95c41b9551bf95e3"><span data-offset-key="0203a9325014488f95c41b9551bf95e3:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/twine" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="606777ca5af64d6f81d7855dc3239149"><span data-offset-key="606777ca5af64d6f81d7855dc3239149:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="c27a59503c1747278ab24562069b0939"><span data-offset-key="c27a59503c1747278ab24562069b0939:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="52e69046ae3b4b01a33c419709cc29a4"><span data-offset-key="52e69046ae3b4b01a33c419709cc29a4:0">Twine is the primary tool developers use to upload packages to the Python Package Index or other Python package indexes. It is a command-line program that passes program files and metadata to a web API. Developers use it because it’s the official PyPI upload tool, it’s fast and secure, it’s maintained, and it reliably works.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5edd82c0119e4166b17332fdcdab4abb"><span data-offset-key="5edd82c0119e4166b17332fdcdab4abb:0">virtualenv</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#virtualenv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="deb6cb07ebbb4d9e96cd601798767d60"><span data-offset-key="deb6cb07ebbb4d9e96cd601798767d60:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="4d42e9d6f6eb4b0986a912ad6ba0eb89"><span data-offset-key="4d42e9d6f6eb4b0986a912ad6ba0eb89:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="800fbb65c2d8408b90b317e1b9685ffe"><span data-offset-key="800fbb65c2d8408b90b317e1b9685ffe:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://virtualenv.pypa.io/en/stable/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c498a37388ec4f50b9c3d5853884d906"><span data-offset-key="c498a37388ec4f50b9c3d5853884d906:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="9652197b0ec447b7bbe5fa36a3f5f38d"><span data-offset-key="9652197b0ec447b7bbe5fa36a3f5f38d:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/virtualenv/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ee46d6317a92464487ef6b4fd6e581f6"><span data-offset-key="ee46d6317a92464487ef6b4fd6e581f6:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="345146116ab442ab9518703d802cb358"><span data-offset-key="345146116ab442ab9518703d802cb358:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/virtualenv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3bef843cd5cd4e14bfc3b6ff08cc6d7f"><span data-offset-key="3bef843cd5cd4e14bfc3b6ff08cc6d7f:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="bd92aeac712947e6ada2f97a930e1718"><span data-offset-key="bd92aeac712947e6ada2f97a930e1718:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/virtualenv/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="58b5b58bab5644ef83371d608cd93a36"><span data-offset-key="58b5b58bab5644ef83371d608cd93a36:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="abfad1e0c8ba45958de3693efc1bd3eb"><span data-offset-key="abfad1e0c8ba45958de3693efc1bd3eb:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6f58640ba8464de4bb14d1ba87f28a6d"><span data-offset-key="6f58640ba8464de4bb14d1ba87f28a6d:0">virtualenv is a tool which uses the command-line path environment variable to create isolated Python </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Virtual-Environment" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="07390a50a4d142d8902f2d12c79b984a"><span data-offset-key="07390a50a4d142d8902f2d12c79b984a:0">Virtual Environments</span></span></a><span data-key="509dbe24986142f9ba32ec2e84dcc0c1"><span data-offset-key="509dbe24986142f9ba32ec2e84dcc0c1:0">, much as </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#venv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0adaeb1261964b89ad060f9eaf61ce9e"><span data-offset-key="0adaeb1261964b89ad060f9eaf61ce9e:0">venv</span></span></a><span data-key="84997d2cf63b452fa3216475eee0135b"><span data-offset-key="84997d2cf63b452fa3216475eee0135b:0"> does. virtualenv provides additional functionality, compared to </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#venv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2a3e435840d24892a56e1453af2e9167"><span data-offset-key="2a3e435840d24892a56e1453af2e9167:0">venv</span></span></a><span data-key="631365a04f664f47b66222df618c92c4"><span data-offset-key="631365a04f664f47b66222df618c92c4:0">, by supporting Python 2.7 and by providing convenient features for configuring, maintaining, duplicating, and troubleshooting the virtual environments. For more information, see the section on </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/tutorials/installing-packages/#creating-and-using-virtual-environments" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="40511cd757cb4bd7b4db6b331e5b298d"><span data-offset-key="40511cd757cb4bd7b4db6b331e5b298d:0">Creating Virtual Environments</span></span></a><span data-key="df57febcca9b4817b4244f3af971626e"><span data-offset-key="df57febcca9b4817b4244f3af971626e:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="73684bd121ee45d882cdf2c3e9fd158d"><span data-offset-key="73684bd121ee45d882cdf2c3e9fd158d:0">Primarily, the wheel project offers the </span><span data-offset-key="73684bd121ee45d882cdf2c3e9fd158d:1">`bdist_wheel`</span><span data-offset-key="73684bd121ee45d882cdf2c3e9fd158d:2"> </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="048aeb92084f4ed895799db8f9c094c3"><span data-offset-key="048aeb92084f4ed895799db8f9c094c3:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="1f87b210fd214aa693bd765de24aaf73"><span data-offset-key="1f87b210fd214aa693bd765de24aaf73:0"> extension for creating </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Wheel" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="78bce8c8984745dabbc01604b76a4ece"><span data-offset-key="78bce8c8984745dabbc01604b76a4ece:0">wheel distributions</span></span></a><span data-key="6aff717edefc4e2dab1f841c2632ec8f"><span data-offset-key="6aff717edefc4e2dab1f841c2632ec8f:0">. Additionally, it offers its own command line utility for creating and installing wheels.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7adfd0abd14f47f0a6f6227ec97b1038"><span data-offset-key="7adfd0abd14f47f0a6f6227ec97b1038:0">See also </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypa/auditwheel" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="939f79b837f04ff1b333078e63a5d062"><span data-offset-key="939f79b837f04ff1b333078e63a5d062:0">auditwheel</span></span></a><span data-key="db56cf23c93e4f488d2fae2f6de13d1e"><span data-offset-key="db56cf23c93e4f488d2fae2f6de13d1e:0">, a tool that package developers use to check and fix Python packages they are making in the binary wheel format. It provides functionality to discover dependencies, check metadata for compliance, and repair the wheel and metadata to properly link and include external shared libraries in a package.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3c80d11c9e7e4e68a100c331b20fcd0f"><span data-offset-key="3c80d11c9e7e4e68a100c331b20fcd0f:0">Non-PyPA Projects</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#non-pypa-projects" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6e978f02a42047548b84a6b25f796685"><span data-offset-key="6e978f02a42047548b84a6b25f796685:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="e49130ab981e473db6c221962da677a4"><span data-offset-key="e49130ab981e473db6c221962da677a4:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>
