<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e585ae64cf42427c81b40ae07c63232a"><span data-offset-key="e585ae64cf42427c81b40ae07c63232a:0">buildout</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#buildout" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="90968a93ab0a48e9a5ced74649087eff"><span data-offset-key="90968a93ab0a48e9a5ced74649087eff:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="46083629498d41f6b7934d236f3939ee"><span data-offset-key="46083629498d41f6b7934d236f3939ee:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b55bbe5465b84e5e941df7e99f35a212"><span data-offset-key="b55bbe5465b84e5e941df7e99f35a212:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="http://www.buildout.org/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="337869f3bb0a4bc3a743d92162a159a9"><span data-offset-key="337869f3bb0a4bc3a743d92162a159a9:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="007d3e16c3ed4d2c82e87254914fb604"><span data-offset-key="007d3e16c3ed4d2c82e87254914fb604:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://bugs.launchpad.net/zc.buildout" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c9e24225d8c541f38fee20f145a05222"><span data-offset-key="c9e24225d8c541f38fee20f145a05222:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="b026d6f2f1af4ccbbf9f30da4a3b4a41"><span data-offset-key="b026d6f2f1af4ccbbf9f30da4a3b4a41:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/zc.buildout" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="52d49c4b193a47c7b395f72d9b8b3f0b"><span data-offset-key="52d49c4b193a47c7b395f72d9b8b3f0b:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="b1fac6040e3e41218beb7918e9dc7340"><span data-offset-key="b1fac6040e3e41218beb7918e9dc7340:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/buildout/buildout/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fd7a0b99956d43cb8b76a11b49d4f19d"><span data-offset-key="fd7a0b99956d43cb8b76a11b49d4f19d:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="1d57d2f5a386443a8c56f4b570308d88"><span data-offset-key="1d57d2f5a386443a8c56f4b570308d88:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="cd75fde108494d95bfd75c6e052cce0d"><span data-offset-key="cd75fde108494d95bfd75c6e052cce0d:0">Buildout is a Python-based build system for creating, assembling and deploying applications from multiple parts, some of which may be non-Python-based. It lets you create a buildout configuration and reproduce the same software later.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b49c043d0cd54fdd981367269df9e1fc"><span data-offset-key="b49c043d0cd54fdd981367269df9e1fc:0">conda</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#conda" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="43ca63c4bc6f41468789233c507a4c8b"><span data-offset-key="43ca63c4bc6f41468789233c507a4c8b:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="63505d4ac8014301bceea03cb3739478"><span data-offset-key="63505d4ac8014301bceea03cb3739478:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bc115fbccda248c58b7bd3dd9e3b031c"><span data-offset-key="bc115fbccda248c58b7bd3dd9e3b031c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="http://conda.pydata.org/docs/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9f12650f9dfa486bbfbd03261ec3cdd4"><span data-offset-key="9f12650f9dfa486bbfbd03261ec3cdd4:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="df8ea97caafc4b84addd453a380f3760"><span data-offset-key="df8ea97caafc4b84addd453a380f3760:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7bbbd6acf0894095ae9bc16efe985627"><span data-offset-key="7bbbd6acf0894095ae9bc16efe985627:0">conda is the package management tool for </span></span><a href="https://docs.anaconda.com/anaconda/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3b0de0c9b46540ec80160d8628593dcf"><span data-offset-key="3b0de0c9b46540ec80160d8628593dcf:0">Anaconda</span></span></a><span data-key="52d3ca2f1514430bac65f6f054c1349b"><span data-offset-key="52d3ca2f1514430bac65f6f054c1349b:0"> Python installations. Anaconda Python is a distribution from </span></span><a href="https://www.anaconda.com/download" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3e484a4de0544f6091a7c8872f0203cf"><span data-offset-key="3e484a4de0544f6091a7c8872f0203cf:0">Anaconda, Inc</span></span></a><span data-key="936f96a46a304029b99321d6a042e3e6"><span data-offset-key="936f96a46a304029b99321d6a042e3e6:0"> specifically aimed at the scientific community, and in particular on Windows where the installation of binary extensions is often difficult.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f7143600c1ab4c8ea11dcce91abe56ef"><span data-offset-key="f7143600c1ab4c8ea11dcce91abe56ef:0">Conda is a completely separate tool from </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6a5f6908f31743c9bd0a9cc10505daff"><span data-offset-key="6a5f6908f31743c9bd0a9cc10505daff:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="e1ad691993c442bcb04de7219b0cc2dd"><span data-offset-key="e1ad691993c442bcb04de7219b0cc2dd:0">, virtualenv and wheel, but provides many of their combined features in terms of package management, virtual environment management and deployment of binary extensions.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e6cf8b40f31d41f8ae5997cc582eb7ce"><span data-offset-key="e6cf8b40f31d41f8ae5997cc582eb7ce:0">Conda does not install packages from PyPI and can install only from the official Anaconda repositories, or anaconda.org (a place for user-contributed </span><span data-offset-key="e6cf8b40f31d41f8ae5997cc582eb7ce:1">_conda_</span><span data-offset-key="e6cf8b40f31d41f8ae5997cc582eb7ce:2"> packages), or a local (e.g. intranet) package server. However, note that </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="30c8801059524d48afeb90549ec1c6c7"><span data-offset-key="30c8801059524d48afeb90549ec1c6c7:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="1103835b024f4be59667da714a5e0026"><span data-offset-key="1103835b024f4be59667da714a5e0026:0"> can be installed into, and work side-by-side with conda for managing </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Distribution-Package" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d671af522356468c875d6efa3defa9fb"><span data-offset-key="d671af522356468c875d6efa3defa9fb:0">distributions</span></span></a><span data-key="73dec645ceb94bd2a44c701e5ff35829"><span data-offset-key="73dec645ceb94bd2a44c701e5ff35829:0"> from PyPI. Also, </span></span><a href="https://docs.conda.io/projects/conda-build/en/latest/user-guide/tutorials/build-pkgs-skeleton.html" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3147216a800b401b934233b88b7f2b04"><span data-offset-key="3147216a800b401b934233b88b7f2b04:0">conda skeleton</span></span></a><span data-key="51422a31c6c74de3a349b99ecfc9d135"><span data-offset-key="51422a31c6c74de3a349b99ecfc9d135:0"> is a tool to make Python packages installable by conda by first fetching them from PyPI and modifying their metadata.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e63ac01d42ad451e9a319346c7c742dd"><span data-offset-key="e63ac01d42ad451e9a319346c7c742dd:0">devpi</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#devpi" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="842a1eacc8254e6da9cc8356ea64b1cb"><span data-offset-key="842a1eacc8254e6da9cc8356ea64b1cb:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="e26ee6d5749845e6b2e67d6f2448f60a"><span data-offset-key="e26ee6d5749845e6b2e67d6f2448f60a:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="02c470221f00426e82ec6368a03e00ae"><span data-offset-key="02c470221f00426e82ec6368a03e00ae:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="http://doc.devpi.net/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5bd8fe35eea548adbc385e6d0238f0ed"><span data-offset-key="5bd8fe35eea548adbc385e6d0238f0ed:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="cc25e3bcf445458e8a5b6fcfea0a5b83"><span data-offset-key="cc25e3bcf445458e8a5b6fcfea0a5b83:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://bitbucket.org/hpk42/devpi/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="460ce982dd564709a9e22685dbc4be0f"><span data-offset-key="460ce982dd564709a9e22685dbc4be0f:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="467a78f586ac40b69b277b32cb3491f0"><span data-offset-key="467a78f586ac40b69b277b32cb3491f0:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/devpi" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e2fe3dff80cd4f5f82189b69a27ff8d1"><span data-offset-key="e2fe3dff80cd4f5f82189b69a27ff8d1:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="a80fe20e6d9c4adea711c420b2fabfcf"><span data-offset-key="a80fe20e6d9c4adea711c420b2fabfcf:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="31136a54c5bc45ac8c58d53ffb769fbc"><span data-offset-key="31136a54c5bc45ac8c58d53ffb769fbc:0">devpi features a powerful PyPI-compatible server and PyPI proxy cache with a complementary command line tool to drive packaging, testing and release activities with Python. devpi also provides a browsable and searchable web interface.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0fc1b0221e924f2688f6d12c47b018f5"><span data-offset-key="0fc1b0221e924f2688f6d12c47b018f5:0">flit</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#flit" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="09a5baa3ce174d93a20293c6417da9dd"><span data-offset-key="09a5baa3ce174d93a20293c6417da9dd:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="9cd574a435ef447fba38cc577f66ca0d"><span data-offset-key="9cd574a435ef447fba38cc577f66ca0d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4d3e6a79c48644d5bb32cbcaf14c885b"><span data-offset-key="4d3e6a79c48644d5bb32cbcaf14c885b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://flit.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="48494b8ddabd4f7e9b011b0a1cbd9d0c"><span data-offset-key="48494b8ddabd4f7e9b011b0a1cbd9d0c:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="8cb0958f8fe5407782037909dd606e02"><span data-offset-key="8cb0958f8fe5407782037909dd606e02:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/takluyver/flit/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1585c8f8449e47d69dede6003d4de25d"><span data-offset-key="1585c8f8449e47d69dede6003d4de25d:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="71ecb8e3e4b54de09c0f1eb377519c45"><span data-offset-key="71ecb8e3e4b54de09c0f1eb377519c45:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/flit" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c621b5ba1a27443b89be4623accc0191"><span data-offset-key="c621b5ba1a27443b89be4623accc0191:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="f391370dce6c48d382aa2d6bbaa0105c"><span data-offset-key="f391370dce6c48d382aa2d6bbaa0105c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="3aee6ef5e2254195907bfd056ba555c0"><span data-offset-key="3aee6ef5e2254195907bfd056ba555c0:0">Flit provides a simple way to upload pure Python packages and modules to PyPI. It focuses on </span></span><a href="https://flit.readthedocs.io/en/latest/rationale.html" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5eaa115641dc4c61bb9177e775909b5c"><span data-offset-key="5eaa115641dc4c61bb9177e775909b5c:0">making the easy things easy</span></span></a><span data-key="7d56165c96ed4062a4b0ac2641d73155"><span data-offset-key="7d56165c96ed4062a4b0ac2641d73155:0"> for packaging. Flit can generate a configuration file to quickly set up a simple project, build source distributions and wheels, and upload them to PyPI.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a11bd69956d140e1b8555fe01c7ffbb4"><span data-offset-key="a11bd69956d140e1b8555fe01c7ffbb4:0">Flit uses </span><span data-offset-key="a11bd69956d140e1b8555fe01c7ffbb4:1">`pyproject.toml`</span><span data-offset-key="a11bd69956d140e1b8555fe01c7ffbb4:2"> to configure a project. Flit does not rely on tools such as </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="04c23b5166a54ba9ab1229f83451d7c3"><span data-offset-key="04c23b5166a54ba9ab1229f83451d7c3:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="9d0c0221b1b84e119aff495cfb93b015"><span data-offset-key="9d0c0221b1b84e119aff495cfb93b015:0"> to build distributions, or </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#twine" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="db6b0a0470274e50940ea6bad24d4b36"><span data-offset-key="db6b0a0470274e50940ea6bad24d4b36:0">twine</span></span></a><span data-key="87e3ec539714493d97d64bf2bac48c21"><span data-offset-key="87e3ec539714493d97d64bf2bac48c21:0"> to upload them to PyPI. Flit requires Python 3, but you can use it to distribute modules for Python 2, so long as they can be imported on Python 3.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d8e92dd9c63248568f917089736730a9"><span data-offset-key="d8e92dd9c63248568f917089736730a9:0">enscons</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#enscons" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b34e45c554ee4f3283d5467fb3cef884"><span data-offset-key="b34e45c554ee4f3283d5467fb3cef884:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="97a9da6aa2a544ab8b58913c534c504b"><span data-offset-key="97a9da6aa2a544ab8b58913c534c504b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a0fb0e27bc0b4d3384f71723d44ab299"><span data-offset-key="a0fb0e27bc0b4d3384f71723d44ab299:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://bitbucket.org/dholth/enscons/src" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a77667d0793046249aaa801cbbc99b95"><span data-offset-key="a77667d0793046249aaa801cbbc99b95:0">Source</span></span></a><span data-key="23ff762c77d543b5ad8bb80841948ea5"><span data-offset-key="23ff762c77d543b5ad8bb80841948ea5:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://bitbucket.org/dholth/enscons/issues" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2213bfc8c6174198b8da6089a71a1f66"><span data-offset-key="2213bfc8c6174198b8da6089a71a1f66:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="686a56482b51486294183126d7d09325"><span data-offset-key="686a56482b51486294183126d7d09325:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/enscons" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8c124bc230ee4287968a2ae328fe04aa"><span data-offset-key="8c124bc230ee4287968a2ae328fe04aa:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="3a2421f9a4aa4e91a9b06af4026c1e3b"><span data-offset-key="3a2421f9a4aa4e91a9b06af4026c1e3b:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="71ca0bda951b4b9998e1927727f3104f"><span data-offset-key="71ca0bda951b4b9998e1927727f3104f:0">Enscons is a Python packaging tool based on </span></span><a href="http://scons.org/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0632ed49e8e647afb74eaadecf6e6377"><span data-offset-key="0632ed49e8e647afb74eaadecf6e6377:0">SCons</span></span></a><span data-key="dc81f6f64fd44015ad0230384c97dea3"><span data-offset-key="dc81f6f64fd44015ad0230384c97dea3:0">. It builds </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="12c8cf8942be48d1a69585018ad6c0cb"><span data-offset-key="12c8cf8942be48d1a69585018ad6c0cb:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="c7b8fa5c367d4d5fbec33c641914b29e"><span data-offset-key="c7b8fa5c367d4d5fbec33c641914b29e:0">-compatible source distributions and wheels without using distutils or setuptools, including distributions with C extensions. Enscons has a different architecture and philosophy than </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#distutils" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="992d60700df24e5a997c62661d9e70d5"><span data-offset-key="992d60700df24e5a997c62661d9e70d5:0">distutils</span></span></a><span data-key="b473a838aea14040b6c03a74edc03e04"><span data-offset-key="b473a838aea14040b6c03a74edc03e04:0">. Rather than adding build features to a Python packaging system, enscons adds Python packaging to a general purpose build system. Enscons helps you to build sdists that can be automatically built by </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7547b3a4bb90402bab309febf03fbd96"><span data-offset-key="7547b3a4bb90402bab309febf03fbd96:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="6dc496ab143d4aa18a8c2b6d2c498b2a"><span data-offset-key="6dc496ab143d4aa18a8c2b6d2c498b2a:0">, and wheels that are independent of enscons.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c045a257eeae4852a17673671ca20b93"><span data-offset-key="c045a257eeae4852a17673671ca20b93:0">Hashdist</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#hashdist" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="18bb50ad0a2e459298b8374e6e2317be"><span data-offset-key="18bb50ad0a2e459298b8374e6e2317be:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="2db73850eed0423f99b43ac30a081ad4"><span data-offset-key="2db73850eed0423f99b43ac30a081ad4:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="608bd08690a541b2ab6c256a3b28f133"><span data-offset-key="608bd08690a541b2ab6c256a3b28f133:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://hashdist.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fbd5df6079c748f0b1de6fa1ab4dde7f"><span data-offset-key="fbd5df6079c748f0b1de6fa1ab4dde7f:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="e3d8e820d0504d22a5622abf4db94d45"><span data-offset-key="e3d8e820d0504d22a5622abf4db94d45:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/hashdist/hashdist/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cbbc434718534f628b559bd9e7c38793"><span data-offset-key="cbbc434718534f628b559bd9e7c38793:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="a420537c998e43b2b6c04badb9bf0659"><span data-offset-key="a420537c998e43b2b6c04badb9bf0659:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ae77259e91354ed5a1e6083da1cc9dfb"><span data-offset-key="ae77259e91354ed5a1e6083da1cc9dfb:0">Hashdist is a library for building non-root software distributions. Hashdist is trying to be “the Debian of choice for cases where Debian technology doesn’t work”. The best way for Pythonistas to think about Hashdist may be a more powerful hybrid of </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#virtualenv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6f2e562cb830490fb3d2c4e861af7c7e"><span data-offset-key="6f2e562cb830490fb3d2c4e861af7c7e:0">virtualenv</span></span></a><span data-key="33c7ec5439534fa691423f037c020a63"><span data-offset-key="33c7ec5439534fa691423f037c020a63:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#buildout" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2e1c38f8383446cfa2f336ea3dfc9775"><span data-offset-key="2e1c38f8383446cfa2f336ea3dfc9775:0">buildout</span></span></a><span data-key="a498cc0856c04c36a79b76162461bef0"><span data-offset-key="a498cc0856c04c36a79b76162461bef0:0">. It is aimed at solving the problem of installing scientific software, and making package distribution stateless, cached, and branchable. It is used by some researchers but has been lacking in maintenance since 2016.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7f489348ad814444a12fb657cb40dd5d"><span data-offset-key="7f489348ad814444a12fb657cb40dd5d:0">hatch</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#hatch" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8e7dfd7e6d444a96b6ae00b7d6d476da"><span data-offset-key="8e7dfd7e6d444a96b6ae00b7d6d476da:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="4b522744db21493e8f30aa5635ca876f"><span data-offset-key="4b522744db21493e8f30aa5635ca876f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0820918b04ba42dd9462fb1b488f7c60"><span data-offset-key="0820918b04ba42dd9462fb1b488f7c60:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/ofek/hatch" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="eccdf85248fd4c03bd521c53d0d794d3"><span data-offset-key="eccdf85248fd4c03bd521c53d0d794d3:0">GitHub and Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="1aae4750e8544552964410d9b14b1572"><span data-offset-key="1aae4750e8544552964410d9b14b1572:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/hatch" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3b1cc2f74c6341d2b0d9c68aa81d7ab0"><span data-offset-key="3b1cc2f74c6341d2b0d9c68aa81d7ab0:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="7731ed8f1a594093bd757736898e7e81"><span data-offset-key="7731ed8f1a594093bd757736898e7e81:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f94bc2b70fff485d8150d26b76e50824"><span data-offset-key="f94bc2b70fff485d8150d26b76e50824:0">Hatch is a unified command-line tool meant to conveniently manage dependencies and environment isolation for Python developers. Python package developers use Hatch to configure, version, specify dependencies for, and publish packages to PyPI. Under the hood, it uses </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#twine" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5d360071295f4753a0f1b54c24d7960e"><span data-offset-key="5d360071295f4753a0f1b54c24d7960e:0">twine</span></span></a><span data-key="39531e173b01418b9ed0686c2026f12d"><span data-offset-key="39531e173b01418b9ed0686c2026f12d:0"> to upload packages to PyPI, and </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7af66e5ade364d39bff7931386563354"><span data-offset-key="7af66e5ade364d39bff7931386563354:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="9b01781dde7b486a8ae4f06a4da691b1"><span data-offset-key="9b01781dde7b486a8ae4f06a4da691b1:0"> to download and install packages.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="927e508d021641f09698e882c092c078"><span data-offset-key="927e508d021641f09698e882c092c078:0">multibuild</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#multibuild" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="01e4a7fe37e04871b4ab5e2b81696c92"><span data-offset-key="01e4a7fe37e04871b4ab5e2b81696c92:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="f538c8e6af0f4aac955f94ca2d9cc853"><span data-offset-key="f538c8e6af0f4aac955f94ca2d9cc853:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="71eabd859342401ea7a821eec7b6aba3"><span data-offset-key="71eabd859342401ea7a821eec7b6aba3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/matthew-brett/multibuild" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="36493f00385e4d3481c886f45d52025f"><span data-offset-key="36493f00385e4d3481c886f45d52025f:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="971cfae483b349e99ed5e11abc803109"><span data-offset-key="971cfae483b349e99ed5e11abc803109:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f7b7533b820248ba9b32150c51c8dcc9"><span data-offset-key="f7b7533b820248ba9b32150c51c8dcc9:0">Multibuild is a set of CI scripts for building and testing Python </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Wheel" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="745ffae5444343f19918accbbc6aa081"><span data-offset-key="745ffae5444343f19918accbbc6aa081:0">wheels</span></span></a><span data-key="f7a9d116f9e142e79044c85825fbbe18"><span data-offset-key="f7a9d116f9e142e79044c85825fbbe18:0"> for Linux, macOS, and (less flexibly) Windows. Also see </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#cibuildwheel" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="57f79257f22a40f897f9e85bf55acf71"><span data-offset-key="57f79257f22a40f897f9e85bf55acf71:0">cibuildwheel</span></span></a><span data-key="1f52861822ba4e66858217859228e55d"><span data-offset-key="1f52861822ba4e66858217859228e55d:0">.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="de24630095464850aa7f32909e00fe90"><span data-offset-key="de24630095464850aa7f32909e00fe90:0">pex</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="041bc7bfe143439c932092aa62d119ff"><span data-offset-key="041bc7bfe143439c932092aa62d119ff:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="7f2b4fd33ba54c488ef65a07c1b7a384"><span data-offset-key="7f2b4fd33ba54c488ef65a07c1b7a384:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="07ab84175e8148219e9deb83e83d2d15"><span data-offset-key="07ab84175e8148219e9deb83e83d2d15:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://pex.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="34ccaf6a870d422394052eee934c1051"><span data-offset-key="34ccaf6a870d422394052eee934c1051:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="7c05e225e4b64a02a8002b992b914a9b"><span data-offset-key="7c05e225e4b64a02a8002b992b914a9b:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pantsbuild/pex/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a0a3051642f446448998dd0f316aaf1d"><span data-offset-key="a0a3051642f446448998dd0f316aaf1d:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="8c5000f66fdf4bc3a54bef9cb556f4bb"><span data-offset-key="8c5000f66fdf4bc3a54bef9cb556f4bb:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/pex" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ad617fc3ced44f2cbdaa4dcf26496b8e"><span data-offset-key="ad617fc3ced44f2cbdaa4dcf26496b8e:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="2e2267c77357417e8fd598f5c9d2cc53"><span data-offset-key="2e2267c77357417e8fd598f5c9d2cc53:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ed651173fe71454683238eb1baa02d11"><span data-offset-key="ed651173fe71454683238eb1baa02d11:0">pex is both a library and tool for generating </span><span data-offset-key="ed651173fe71454683238eb1baa02d11:1">`.pex`</span><span data-offset-key="ed651173fe71454683238eb1baa02d11:2"> (Python EXecutable) files, standalone Python environments in the spirit of </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#virtualenv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e9ec600402804ff78b222304cdd0a5b1"><span data-offset-key="e9ec600402804ff78b222304cdd0a5b1:0">virtualenv</span></span></a><span data-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da"><span data-offset-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da:0">. </span><span data-offset-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da:1">`.pex`</span><span data-offset-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da:2"> files are just carefully constructed zip files with a </span><span data-offset-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da:3">`#!/usr/bin/env python`</span><span data-offset-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da:4"> and special </span><span data-offset-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da:5">`__main__.py`</span><span data-offset-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da:6">, and are designed to make deployment of Python applications as simple as </span><span data-offset-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da:7">`cp`</span><span data-offset-key="f1d3c3a8ee3b4f2eb008c10ff3c6f1da:8">.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="995161092a9a42258faf4412b7dfc20a"><span data-offset-key="995161092a9a42258faf4412b7dfc20a:0">pip-tools</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip-tools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5becc8224cee4fd4aea8ecbfd53ac88d"><span data-offset-key="5becc8224cee4fd4aea8ecbfd53ac88d:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="0a1168a52098415891cd11cbbe06a2c8"><span data-offset-key="0a1168a52098415891cd11cbbe06a2c8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9b7709c7f1544e52aabcd41245acdba2"><span data-offset-key="9b7709c7f1544e52aabcd41245acdba2:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/jazzband/pip-tools/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="61b6b81495b44563ad11a3d22786e83c"><span data-offset-key="61b6b81495b44563ad11a3d22786e83c:0">GitHub and Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="b32b358651354b0dac584d5d6a4ab3a8"><span data-offset-key="b32b358651354b0dac584d5d6a4ab3a8:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/pip-tools/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b0e8a74d071649e7bbff4a8641074f81"><span data-offset-key="b0e8a74d071649e7bbff4a8641074f81:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="634853cca0224775b2daef9725e5fd52"><span data-offset-key="634853cca0224775b2daef9725e5fd52:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="81526b87c692405e92bae84a3e615d27"><span data-offset-key="81526b87c692405e92bae84a3e615d27:0">pip-tools is a suite of tools meant for Python system administrators and release managers who particularly want to keep their builds deterministic yet stay up to date with new versions of their dependencies. Users can specify particular release of their dependencies via hash, conveniently make a properly formatted list of requirements from information in other parts of their program, update all dependencies (a feature </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="57ad82cee49c4214b44777c8c72fbcee"><span data-offset-key="57ad82cee49c4214b44777c8c72fbcee:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="be62dee78ccb4fe7b7de6974e65c0a30"><span data-offset-key="be62dee78ccb4fe7b7de6974e65c0a30:0"> currently does not provide), and create layers of constraints for the program to obey.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="374057dd38aa4405a6674f595b927ab0"><span data-offset-key="374057dd38aa4405a6674f595b927ab0:0">piwheels</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#piwheels" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a9c9dfaf9d204249b491012e25454b2a"><span data-offset-key="a9c9dfaf9d204249b491012e25454b2a:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="3f80c157dd2b45589b338679e0a7a635"><span data-offset-key="3f80c157dd2b45589b338679e0a7a635:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5f679a56eb6845bb89db987172789a79"><span data-offset-key="5f679a56eb6845bb89db987172789a79:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://www.piwheels.org/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ef41b1665cf54965906a5a7e10776b21"><span data-offset-key="ef41b1665cf54965906a5a7e10776b21:0">Website</span></span></a><span data-key="040e5f01dc004f43b1962d54b72c3a1b"><span data-offset-key="040e5f01dc004f43b1962d54b72c3a1b:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://piwheels.readthedocs.io/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="9c8879694c804e1e9ac2f0bebcca9317"><span data-offset-key="9c8879694c804e1e9ac2f0bebcca9317:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="d2fcf59b1d79433c9a1a938a1a5a8f2a"><span data-offset-key="d2fcf59b1d79433c9a1a938a1a5a8f2a:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/piwheels/piwheels/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fe2b95998c904c36aeebe84cca0e427d"><span data-offset-key="fe2b95998c904c36aeebe84cca0e427d:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="031cfbe4be494924a3c289173b317c6f"><span data-offset-key="031cfbe4be494924a3c289173b317c6f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ecfc27e05623422c874e26e8bacfc6c2"><span data-offset-key="ecfc27e05623422c874e26e8bacfc6c2:0">piwheels is a website, and software underpinning it, that fetches source code distribution packages from PyPI and compiles them into binary wheels that are optimized for installation onto Raspberry Pi computers. Raspberry Pi OS pre-configures pip to use piwheels.org as an additional index to PyPI.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b54d9390fb9344fea45ad57f1c3d987b"><span data-offset-key="b54d9390fb9344fea45ad57f1c3d987b:0">poetry</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#poetry" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8ffe90d4e9f442cfb66c28c0dfd66dc3"><span data-offset-key="8ffe90d4e9f442cfb66c28c0dfd66dc3:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="81121e8b3a174169b9e8ac81e1f64114"><span data-offset-key="81121e8b3a174169b9e8ac81e1f64114:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f9432751e9964e669fdd32db946a2800"><span data-offset-key="f9432751e9964e669fdd32db946a2800:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://python-poetry.org/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="44dcde8347974ba98e9a248d78b08372"><span data-offset-key="44dcde8347974ba98e9a248d78b08372:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="99a4777d61084f4d943ca2147fb6966b"><span data-offset-key="99a4777d61084f4d943ca2147fb6966b:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/python-poetry/poetry" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d1724ba2f5ce45fd9901ca0858e73fae"><span data-offset-key="d1724ba2f5ce45fd9901ca0858e73fae:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="6b3b16894d7c4c95a42b4d7ffa9d75fb"><span data-offset-key="6b3b16894d7c4c95a42b4d7ffa9d75fb:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/poetry/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="66a565879fdc41f1aa99261d554427c4"><span data-offset-key="66a565879fdc41f1aa99261d554427c4:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="e70114f70a0246c6b89c5299f6971b41"><span data-offset-key="e70114f70a0246c6b89c5299f6971b41:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="639fb36b8fbc4472a121ae47048e3611"><span data-offset-key="639fb36b8fbc4472a121ae47048e3611:0">poetry is a command-line tool to handle dependency installation and isolation as well as building and packaging of Python packages. It uses </span><span data-offset-key="639fb36b8fbc4472a121ae47048e3611:1">`pyproject.toml`</span><span data-offset-key="639fb36b8fbc4472a121ae47048e3611:2"> and, instead of depending on the resolver functionality within </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6ae487b5b01d46a9bb7371d6e6ca52fd"><span data-offset-key="6ae487b5b01d46a9bb7371d6e6ca52fd:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="02cc2c02710943a59d7247969d205cf4"><span data-offset-key="02cc2c02710943a59d7247969d205cf4:0">, provides its own dependency resolver. It attempts to speed users’ experience of installation and dependency resolution by locally caching metadata about dependencies.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4c10c5a9e8b6403db80833aa83ab0dc5"><span data-offset-key="4c10c5a9e8b6403db80833aa83ab0dc5:0">pypiserver</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pypiserver" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="aa4c1dd038be435380737ac4aea8b7cb"><span data-offset-key="aa4c1dd038be435380737ac4aea8b7cb:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="3ec7787fca3d48fcab4228698f6265f8"><span data-offset-key="3ec7787fca3d48fcab4228698f6265f8:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8a512ad8b59941678af096dd512f8552"><span data-offset-key="8a512ad8b59941678af096dd512f8552:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypiserver/pypiserver/blob/master/README.rst" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ae2449d5b3824727b59c7865922c0d67"><span data-offset-key="ae2449d5b3824727b59c7865922c0d67:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="d30da7e80c2f4e24a0fe3c732681a192"><span data-offset-key="d30da7e80c2f4e24a0fe3c732681a192:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/pypiserver/pypiserver" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f2d49b41b1934da4b191c09de6014ba2"><span data-offset-key="f2d49b41b1934da4b191c09de6014ba2:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="0aaa91fd6647431db03eb503afc0f727"><span data-offset-key="0aaa91fd6647431db03eb503afc0f727:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/pypiserver/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c27f381ac477402e97f36c4fdb9adbe4"><span data-offset-key="c27f381ac477402e97f36c4fdb9adbe4:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="c0636c8a9dc94c17bdd17f8a8f9040c1"><span data-offset-key="c0636c8a9dc94c17bdd17f8a8f9040c1:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8f9e135ba6954e06b0b2b377047f4a56"><span data-offset-key="8f9e135ba6954e06b0b2b377047f4a56:0">pypiserver is a minimalist application that serves as a private Python package index within organizations, implementing a simple API and browser interface. You can upload private packages using standard upload tools, and users can download and install them with </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e437ea0fa3c64e7f92d2d86059f91c6b"><span data-offset-key="e437ea0fa3c64e7f92d2d86059f91c6b:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="1aa85c8f916a4c0cbf8f59165b3b8b44"><span data-offset-key="1aa85c8f916a4c0cbf8f59165b3b8b44:0">, without publishing them publicly. Organizations who use pypiserver usually download packages both from pypiserver and from PyPI.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9e51c5f6c6254ee7b1a6ea131fa5f312"><span data-offset-key="9e51c5f6c6254ee7b1a6ea131fa5f312:0">scikit-build</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#scikit-build" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2109de3e0b274927939a0b1829df033e"><span data-offset-key="2109de3e0b274927939a0b1829df033e:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="64ae1699cb3b4f12a5c24aa74c70b710"><span data-offset-key="64ae1699cb3b4f12a5c24aa74c70b710:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8742319d12c14c049fc73bbefa55e713"><span data-offset-key="8742319d12c14c049fc73bbefa55e713:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://scikit-build.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d4970c1f644f41e385cb1b37d66168d3"><span data-offset-key="d4970c1f644f41e385cb1b37d66168d3:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="71cec87815c64ec2ab643895383e7c31"><span data-offset-key="71cec87815c64ec2ab643895383e7c31:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/scikit-build/scikit-build/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5dcd908bdf554058af7f2c2c703df302"><span data-offset-key="5dcd908bdf554058af7f2c2c703df302:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="1dec3b4f81694d20873712eedcc7d44a"><span data-offset-key="1dec3b4f81694d20873712eedcc7d44a:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/scikit-build" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5204da106ce14e0dbcb9962d3439c92b"><span data-offset-key="5204da106ce14e0dbcb9962d3439c92b:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="c2c964022dbd46c4b8b72383b434f67e"><span data-offset-key="c2c964022dbd46c4b8b72383b434f67e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c412e6bbe5dd4a27b2229489dbde224e"><span data-offset-key="c412e6bbe5dd4a27b2229489dbde224e:0">Scikit-build is an improved build system generator for CPython C/C++/Fortran/Cython extensions that integrates with </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d1c008bd47374510934fa65e7897e0fd"><span data-offset-key="d1c008bd47374510934fa65e7897e0fd:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="b18c4b2b3e854cf09f4b89e279dbe9c5"><span data-offset-key="b18c4b2b3e854cf09f4b89e279dbe9c5:0">, </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#wheel" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d103f9eaa08e406888111b907cd13c41"><span data-offset-key="d103f9eaa08e406888111b907cd13c41:0">wheel</span></span></a><span data-key="d87e0fdc645e42c88ff054385bd5daf9"><span data-offset-key="d87e0fdc645e42c88ff054385bd5daf9:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b5a99520533b4a3ea2053e487e12aa10"><span data-offset-key="b5a99520533b4a3ea2053e487e12aa10:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="7e74dfa285bb4e86b15d1f6562f75832"><span data-offset-key="7e74dfa285bb4e86b15d1f6562f75832:0">. It internally uses </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/cmake" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="7902f253fbc4481693afe8e377544830"><span data-offset-key="7902f253fbc4481693afe8e377544830:0">cmake</span></span></a><span data-key="43b513b8dded447eacb9d3ace3880a94"><span data-offset-key="43b513b8dded447eacb9d3ace3880a94:0"> (available on PyPI) to provide better support for additional compilers, build systems, cross compilation, and locating dependencies and their associated build requirements. To speed up and parallelize the build of large projects, the user can install </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/ninja" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c74bb84d55da43b2874dc170dbc30e69"><span data-offset-key="c74bb84d55da43b2874dc170dbc30e69:0">ninja</span></span></a><span data-key="c9328e1c82334b8f8390768efbeb745c"><span data-offset-key="c9328e1c82334b8f8390768efbeb745c:0"> (also available on PyPI).</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8076b1dd56e148aaaeda388e9cde43a7"><span data-offset-key="8076b1dd56e148aaaeda388e9cde43a7:0">shiv</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#shiv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e13e95775ee5486ba2606c59dcd632b7"><span data-offset-key="e13e95775ee5486ba2606c59dcd632b7:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="cced662cb51d4205b94e7e571810717d"><span data-offset-key="cced662cb51d4205b94e7e571810717d:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a0be6dd2329740a1a2d7d3bce139e445"><span data-offset-key="a0be6dd2329740a1a2d7d3bce139e445:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://shiv.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f0773e662a974b04a032c7940339049f"><span data-offset-key="f0773e662a974b04a032c7940339049f:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="389b0f0a500c4a72bf8b2233f3fb666a"><span data-offset-key="389b0f0a500c4a72bf8b2233f3fb666a:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/linkedin/shiv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e4a2c12449e34039a54ca6416ca9738f"><span data-offset-key="e4a2c12449e34039a54ca6416ca9738f:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="caa337b9e2dd40408777a05888f2fe7b"><span data-offset-key="caa337b9e2dd40408777a05888f2fe7b:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/shiv/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b0e895e16fa048dcbfea720e3d655765"><span data-offset-key="b0e895e16fa048dcbfea720e3d655765:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="724748e7bfa54d26893f9ecccfc2d000"><span data-offset-key="724748e7bfa54d26893f9ecccfc2d000:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="447779083689467988d3d046dd64fff3"><span data-offset-key="447779083689467988d3d046dd64fff3:0">shiv is a command line utility for building fully self contained Python zipapps as outlined in </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0441" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="5b8dbb37793a4b82b2956e577c96b043"><span data-offset-key="5b8dbb37793a4b82b2956e577c96b043:0"><strong>PEP 441</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="f61875e9368d4c71b4a9075c27180b55"><span data-offset-key="f61875e9368d4c71b4a9075c27180b55:0">, but with all their dependencies included. Its primary goal is making distributing Python applications and command line tools fast & easy.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="318adcde920945079148ce48b352818d"><span data-offset-key="318adcde920945079148ce48b352818d:0">Spack</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#spack" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f211d5aad6de40a492481a9b095d44e8"><span data-offset-key="f211d5aad6de40a492481a9b095d44e8:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="d5eed6a100c0453da40453326d87f096"><span data-offset-key="d5eed6a100c0453da40453326d87f096:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f1db367ceb004ea59a0e15898eebd76f"><span data-offset-key="f1db367ceb004ea59a0e15898eebd76f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://spack.readthedocs.io/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="03bb9d11afb249d38fa514ea4b12bf4b"><span data-offset-key="03bb9d11afb249d38fa514ea4b12bf4b:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="5b49f5b02f3b41ccaaac754456c6c3af"><span data-offset-key="5b49f5b02f3b41ccaaac754456c6c3af:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/llnl/spack/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1da00afb61ad4ed39ff78aaf6c633715"><span data-offset-key="1da00afb61ad4ed39ff78aaf6c633715:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="bb0366e4ebd042f1ba96501a82f7df87"><span data-offset-key="bb0366e4ebd042f1ba96501a82f7df87:0"> | </span></span><a href="http://www.computer.org/csdl/proceedings/sc/2015/3723/00/2807623.pdf" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f16cb77c77c545039ffc8a61e02a8c98"><span data-offset-key="f16cb77c77c545039ffc8a61e02a8c98:0">Paper</span></span></a><span data-key="7aa5069cad734e90a5846682479f4b7b"><span data-offset-key="7aa5069cad734e90a5846682479f4b7b:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://tgamblin.github.io/files/Gamblin-Spack-SC15-Talk.pdf" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="88908b9b74984654a9b180660584830a"><span data-offset-key="88908b9b74984654a9b180660584830a:0">Slides</span></span></a><span data-key="94cba4f3ce5e4cef9a6daf1a5d544391"><span data-offset-key="94cba4f3ce5e4cef9a6daf1a5d544391:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="42fc0c879cbb43b6978870038b0739da"><span data-offset-key="42fc0c879cbb43b6978870038b0739da:0">A flexible package manager designed to support multiple versions, configurations, platforms, and compilers. Spack is like Homebrew, but packages are written in Python and parameterized to allow easy swapping of compilers, library versions, build options, etc. Arbitrarily many versions of packages can coexist on the same system. Spack was designed for rapidly building high performance scientific applications on clusters and supercomputers.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="65c271e90d214995a363174d43a16906"><span data-offset-key="65c271e90d214995a363174d43a16906:0">Spack is not in PyPI (yet), but it requires no installation and can be used immediately after cloning from GitHub.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6441b6b1c8c9438389964d48340335f2"><span data-offset-key="6441b6b1c8c9438389964d48340335f2:0">zest.releaser</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#zest-releaser" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="574dca8cabac407cb877a13a0826222f"><span data-offset-key="574dca8cabac407cb877a13a0826222f:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="12dbb7e97ff74eec835a52d7791ab18f"><span data-offset-key="12dbb7e97ff74eec835a52d7791ab18f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7db091018f5144b19c49d56837ec965e"><span data-offset-key="7db091018f5144b19c49d56837ec965e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://zestreleaser.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0352078bff574212acb677ab9b6969b6"><span data-offset-key="0352078bff574212acb677ab9b6969b6:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="da112e2d97774ffda7ad06d121c1c211"><span data-offset-key="da112e2d97774ffda7ad06d121c1c211:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://github.com/zestsoftware/zest.releaser/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="6f4d35793c49486aa3b2e777a9508e60"><span data-offset-key="6f4d35793c49486aa3b2e777a9508e60:0">GitHub</span></span></a><span data-key="96366c99b5cd47828a1dbf2800f6748f"><span data-offset-key="96366c99b5cd47828a1dbf2800f6748f:0"> | </span></span><a href="https://pypi.org/project/zest.releaser/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1129e85c0833476faa04c37b701e7f4e"><span data-offset-key="1129e85c0833476faa04c37b701e7f4e:0">PyPI</span></span></a><span data-key="1e3a6e0439ea443cb6c6e9d9ec74f689"><span data-offset-key="1e3a6e0439ea443cb6c6e9d9ec74f689:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ea58d9c9de444f929ed0f98b9656fe0a"><span data-offset-key="ea58d9c9de444f929ed0f98b9656fe0a:0">`zest.releaser`</span><span data-offset-key="ea58d9c9de444f929ed0f98b9656fe0a:1"> is a Python package release tool providing an abstraction layer on top of </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#twine" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d3d65d4623e94c9a83d748bdb2e97073"><span data-offset-key="d3d65d4623e94c9a83d748bdb2e97073:0">twine</span></span></a><span data-key="bd53a8d1b6fd4443bdf7fadf83841018"><span data-offset-key="bd53a8d1b6fd4443bdf7fadf83841018:0">. Python developers use </span><span data-offset-key="bd53a8d1b6fd4443bdf7fadf83841018:1">`zest.releaser`</span><span data-offset-key="bd53a8d1b6fd4443bdf7fadf83841018:2"> to automate incrementing package version numbers, updating changelogs, tagging releases in source control, and uploading new packages to PyPI.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH600-23f228db--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="267a5b7aae104ac297cfedd4ba785971"><span data-offset-key="267a5b7aae104ac297cfedd4ba785971:0">Standard Library Projects</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#standard-library-projects" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2238dbe759c649b18ccef98fb576d34a"><span data-offset-key="2238dbe759c649b18ccef98fb576d34a:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="7c2b8ef960b5473da4feb5901855bec3"><span data-offset-key="7c2b8ef960b5473da4feb5901855bec3:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2e9dddb701ec4a5c8978b0ad271bf62c"><span data-offset-key="2e9dddb701ec4a5c8978b0ad271bf62c:0">ensurepip</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#ensurepip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f046d48dbdba497ba2187493145b6837"><span data-offset-key="f046d48dbdba497ba2187493145b6837:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="0e82a2e08f264b6faa8cadae2a1eac0c"><span data-offset-key="0e82a2e08f264b6faa8cadae2a1eac0c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ec1d3a8bb7df4b668df7d05fa965dd42"><span data-offset-key="ec1d3a8bb7df4b668df7d05fa965dd42:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/ensurepip.html" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="62ca31a64b7740fab05b22e78cdfacfa"><span data-offset-key="62ca31a64b7740fab05b22e78cdfacfa:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="5da65f72b32445d29b499e93b99b608f"><span data-offset-key="5da65f72b32445d29b499e93b99b608f:0"> | </span></span><a href="http://bugs.python.org/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="a660520a213d4c46bc802e1d1edb8002"><span data-offset-key="a660520a213d4c46bc802e1d1edb8002:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="e069da63ffec4a59a7fe2dc2685a707f"><span data-offset-key="e069da63ffec4a59a7fe2dc2685a707f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="11edc8de415346d4bfcebafc9cb343b3"><span data-offset-key="11edc8de415346d4bfcebafc9cb343b3:0">A package in the Python Standard Library that provides support for bootstrapping </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#pip" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="819dff752f4a481184b0cd5c10812d3e"><span data-offset-key="819dff752f4a481184b0cd5c10812d3e:0">pip</span></span></a><span data-key="26ef8de41ee444c998cefb462f3983eb"><span data-offset-key="26ef8de41ee444c998cefb462f3983eb:0"> into an existing Python installation or virtual environment. In most cases, end users won’t use this module, but rather it will be used during the build of the Python distribution.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ea8bede2f3fa4ab5adc9ba1f276e9a86"><span data-offset-key="ea8bede2f3fa4ab5adc9ba1f276e9a86:0">distutils</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#distutils" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cc925dad659e4a298ccf3f697fdc3cac"><span data-offset-key="cc925dad659e4a298ccf3f697fdc3cac:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="a26086b05c26428b92dd8509aeafc827"><span data-offset-key="a26086b05c26428b92dd8509aeafc827:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="45cc65d1c8254e2394d6882fb67cc786"><span data-offset-key="45cc65d1c8254e2394d6882fb67cc786:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/distutils.html" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1b79f286443d4f36acff53a96a58bbc6"><span data-offset-key="1b79f286443d4f36acff53a96a58bbc6:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="b1bd270ba5e3468e9240b82d42ffa4d1"><span data-offset-key="b1bd270ba5e3468e9240b82d42ffa4d1:0"> | </span></span><a href="http://bugs.python.org/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d0d63668cf5e4dd3aedb32e196489f18"><span data-offset-key="d0d63668cf5e4dd3aedb32e196489f18:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="86b19669019049fab40eb45087c2449c"><span data-offset-key="86b19669019049fab40eb45087c2449c:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="176300c9db874bccbced268156b75193"><span data-offset-key="176300c9db874bccbced268156b75193:0">The original Python packaging system, added to the standard library in Python 2.0.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0e326f129c47485196cf392770723498"><span data-offset-key="0e326f129c47485196cf392770723498:0">Due to the challenges of maintaining a packaging system where feature updates are tightly coupled to language runtime updates, direct usage of </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#distutils" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="cbba72842c99400c9e6555f1fb0849b2"><span data-offset-key="cbba72842c99400c9e6555f1fb0849b2:0">distutils</span></span></a><span data-key="9d22731813a94a42ae816a79d3803599"><span data-offset-key="9d22731813a94a42ae816a79d3803599:0"> is now actively discouraged, with </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2dd30154d8094b35894df88a556c9d66"><span data-offset-key="2dd30154d8094b35894df88a556c9d66:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="264b4cc3e2084965aae707aed841746e"><span data-offset-key="264b4cc3e2084965aae707aed841746e:0"> being the preferred replacement. </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#setuptools" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d6378e623656488dbe1b4d10efb78fbe"><span data-offset-key="d6378e623656488dbe1b4d10efb78fbe:0">setuptools</span></span></a><span data-key="78ec3f169b7848e08d63d67045768ab3"><span data-offset-key="78ec3f169b7848e08d63d67045768ab3:0"> not only provides features that plain </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#distutils" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="83b2dff46db54fc3926b9051cff057f9"><span data-offset-key="83b2dff46db54fc3926b9051cff057f9:0">distutils</span></span></a><span data-key="4849ad0456c84a86a803393cf4e6712d"><span data-offset-key="4849ad0456c84a86a803393cf4e6712d:0"> doesn’t offer (such as dependency declarations and entry point declarations), it also provides a consistent build interface and feature set across all supported Python versions.</span></span></span>

###

<span class="text-4505230f--HeadingH400-686c0942--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="24f1a9366e554e2089aa588541a8ab75"><span data-offset-key="24f1a9366e554e2089aa588541a8ab75:0">venv</span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/key_projects/#venv" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="34d9b90ccb9d420da4e315023d6fec46"><span data-offset-key="34d9b90ccb9d420da4e315023d6fec46:0">¶</span></span></a><span data-key="38f82a964bba4c76aa714c65c2f105d9"><span data-offset-key="38f82a964bba4c76aa714c65c2f105d9:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="07e89375072b468cba97377778c382fe"><span data-offset-key="07e89375072b468cba97377778c382fe:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/venv.html" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ef504c6121994a7b9c518e4fbf3ec17c"><span data-offset-key="ef504c6121994a7b9c518e4fbf3ec17c:0">Docs</span></span></a><span data-key="de6a6770abd343bd900d56470af4ab7e"><span data-offset-key="de6a6770abd343bd900d56470af4ab7e:0"> | </span></span><a href="http://bugs.python.org/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8c917e0778b74372918250b5a37121f6"><span data-offset-key="8c917e0778b74372918250b5a37121f6:0">Issues</span></span></a><span data-key="21fa5f26360c4edd8caf18e484a00526"><span data-offset-key="21fa5f26360c4edd8caf18e484a00526:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a41feaa9b4c24e0faadeb5903f6a1862"><span data-offset-key="a41feaa9b4c24e0faadeb5903f6a1862:0">A package in the Python Standard Library (starting with Python 3.3) for creating </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/glossary/#term-Virtual-Environment" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bb80f5c441ea4de7b4ade4b785242e28"><span data-offset-key="bb80f5c441ea4de7b4ade4b785242e28:0">Virtual Environments</span></span></a><span data-key="e4f38177f294483aadc68cac0d891ea6"><span data-offset-key="e4f38177f294483aadc68cac0d891ea6:0">. For more information, see the section on </span></span><a href="https://packaging.python.org/tutorials/installing-packages/#creating-and-using-virtual-environments" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b5b1ec8b6813494d8590d31c23ec936b"><span data-offset-key="b5b1ec8b6813494d8590d31c23ec936b:0">Creating Virtual Environments</span></span></a><span data-key="99c88ebe39604738aa203a6ff34e4fb4"><span data-offset-key="99c88ebe39604738aa203a6ff34e4fb4:0">.</span></span></span>
